250 VII 20 A Bayside held nine executive committee meetings and nine general member ship meetings.
251 VII 20 B Bayside had a new member rendezvous on July 29, 2007 on Little Neck Bay.

Bayside had a raft-up on August 19, 2007 on Manhasset Bay (Leeds Pond).
252 VII 20 C Bayside had four observers.

A report was submitted for a mid-channel buoy that was removed from LIttle Neck Bay.
253 VII 20 D Bayside members attended the Tri-District rendezvous (Districts 2, 3 & 4) at Liberty Landing, NJ from July 6, 2007 - July 8, 2008.

Bayside members attended District 3 Rendezvous East in Norwich. Connecticut from August 4, 2007 to August 6, 2007.  Three boats represented Bayside.

Bayside member attended three council meetings, the Fall Educational Conference and the Spring Conference.
254 VII 20 E Bayside members attended the governing board in Norfolk, Virginia and the Annual Meeting in Dallas, Texas.
255 VII 20 F Bayside attended the Holiday Party of the Poppenhussen Institute in College Point.
256 VII 20 G There are two members certified as vessel safety inspectors.  They conducted a total of 12 vessel safety checks.

Pat and Dick Jarmon were very invovled in the organizing committee and many members participated in making table centerpieces, greeting attendees, staffing tables at events, and acting as guides at the venue.

1 Online Blog Opens <p>
	Online Blog opens to promote 100th Anniversary events.</p> 2012-04-30 http://www.usps.org/php/100 M Y N Y E147948 <p>
	A specially developed &quot;blog&quot; has been created to allow squadorns and districts to share their 100th Anniversary Celebrations.</p>
2 100th Anniversary ENSIGN Unveiled <p>
	The<span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 205);"><strong> Flag and Etiquette Committee </strong></span>has approved a special ensign to be used for the 100th anniversary. It may only be flown from 2013-2014, and then it will be retired.</p>
<p>
	All Districts in USPS will receive a commemorative ensign at the 2013 Annual Meeting in Jacksonville. District commanders will take the ensign back to their respective districts to use throughout the year. Squadrons will be able to order a special ribbon to be designed by its members according to the flag company&rsquo;s specifications. When completed, it will be attached to their District 100th anniversary ensign. All ribbons and ensigns will return to Jacksonville in 2014 and be part of a special flag ceremony during the opening ceremonies of the Governing Board Meeting on Saturday morning.</p>
<p>

21 pgm_21 Member Email Checker 0 init_16 estatus.pl /web/bin/cgi-bin-tools// server last checked certificate number in mbftp seed reco 5 15600 E105868 batch perl USPS_WebServerEmailProcessiong.doc Cycles through all member records rechecking 4000 emails a night for validity.

This uses a Perl MOD which works by emulating a mail server and establishing a session with the server for the email address in question. Perl MODs are user contributed processes shared within the Perl Community.  

This process uses perl mod "Mail::CheckUser" to emulate a mail server and check the validity of an email address.  It cycles through 4000 emails a night rechecking all email addresses several times a month.  If the email address is valid, the estatus field is set to 0 otherwise it is set to one of the following values depending on the problem encountered.  Note a value of 6 is not set by this process.  If the status is different than what it was before, the new value is placed in the mbftp database record and MQSeries is used to send the update to the AS400.  The certificate number of the last email address checked is stored in the seed record of the mbftp table.  That seed record is fetched with a certificate number key of "0000000". It runs as a crontab entry under ID "dtb". Estatus values will be described later.
Uses estatus field of mbftp to store status as follows
0	Valid
1	DNS Timeout
2	ISP Timeout
3	ISP Unreachable
4	Unknown Error
5	Held/Full/Blocked
6	Rejected by ISP/NS
7	Mailbox Invalid
8	Provider Invalid
9	Format Invalid
There is a hand shake between servers and error status is returned when the email address is invalid.  Just before the actual email content is to be sent the server emulator signals an error and drops the connection.

A status is 1 or 2 indicates that the server emulator was unable to connect with the target mail server and the estatus is actually unknown.  To determine the actual status of the email address a real message is sent to the address which explains that a test is being made to see if the address is real and that there is no need to respond to the message.  If the recipient's server or the network bounces the message it is detected by the "Email Bounce Detector" and processed by the "Email Bounce Processor".  Those email which were rejected for a known reason may have their estatus set to "6" for "Rejected by ISP/Network".

Member Emails with an estatus of "6" are only rechecked once a month when the first new cycle through members begins. 2012-05-15 2013-02-16
14 pgm_14 Make Merit Mark Certificate 0 init_0 makeMMX.php //web/php/DHinders/meritmarks/ server certno supplied through web form 5 11000 E122722 query php Merit Marks.doc Creates the MM certificate in .pdf format.  Uses one of two .jpg files a template for the image. It has been our experience that for a number of members clicking on the link provided in the email message does not work.  Copying and pasting the URL provided may be beyond the expertise of some members, so we have provided a simpler URL (http://tiny.cc/GetMeritMark ) which takes them to a page where they simply enter their certificate number and click on Submit to retrieve their merit mark. 2012-05-09 2013-02-16

78 pgm78 Daily Jobs Load 0 init_16 djobs.pl //web/bin/cgi-bin-tools/ server 8 15000 E105868 batch perl Loads jobs tables with data from HQ Run as a cronjob under ID "dtb".  Actually three scripts batched as part of "nightly.pl".  sjobs.pl which reloads the squadron jobs table "sjftp" from SJFTP.TXT.  djobs.pl which reloads the district jobs table "dcdxo" from DJFTP.TXT.  njobs.pl which reloads the national jobs table "njftp" from NJFTP.TXT. If a new file was not FTPed during the morning the script is aborted.

sjobs.pl has an additional function it assigns acting squadron jobs when they are not defined in the table "sjftp" so that reporting may be done to the squadrons via email or so that there is an individual with the required security available when the need arises.  Currently the only acting job assigned is SEO and if none exists the ASEO is assigned and if no ASEO exists, the Cdr is assigned.  This is table driven and can be expanded to include other jobs.

A SEO is required in order to order educational materials and examinations. 2012-06-20 2013-02-16
30 pgm_30 Daily Squad/Dist Data Sync 0 init_16 SQFTP.pl //web/bin/cgi-bin-tools/ server 8 15000 E105868 batch perl USPS_WebServerEmailProcessiong.doc Checks ftp from HQ against websites
Updated to check IT,PUB, and Roster contacts against jobcodes. Runs under ID "dtb" as a cron entry.  Run nightly.  Bundled as part of "nightly.pl"

156 pgm156 Module - Show Events 0 show_events.php / joomla 15 0 E208009 Joomla 'Module' to display future education and meeting events.  Uses dbUSPSWebSites.php library to access tables in the WebSites database.  
Displays event list in one of several formats as selected by the Joomla administrator. Implemented as a Joomla Module.  Program consists of two distinct PHP files to obtain event or HQ-800 records, and a manifest.xml file that identifies the administration parameters, and several (view) files that package event record contents inot a display format.  At this time there are two view files, 1 to show an event's data as a list of items and one to show the event data on a line. 
On startup the main show_events.php file obtains the squadron or district account code from a Joomla session variable and calls the helper.php file to query database tables an return a list of events.  Then it calls the specified view .php file to format and display the events.

1 mbftp VHQAB server Contains a working list of USPS Members and USPS University Students.  Synchronized daily with the master member roster maintained on the IBM system in Raleigh.
2 mbsasync VHQAB server Contains data on USPS Members sent to SailAngle.com.  Used to manage synchronization.  In addition to the following fields the member's first and last name are sent.

3 ns_marks ns_db server The server based record of awarded Merit Marks.  Used by on-line programs to create a MM PDF file and to display all members who have received electronic merit marks.

Record is added to ns_db.ns_marks to record a members MM status.

12 doc_programs DOC server Master table for data on USPS IT Programs.  Generally there are two types of programs: 
1 - Programs called from an external event such as a member request or a CRONtab job. 
2 - Programs called from other programs

Identity of all 1st level programs is essential.  Otherwise searching to identify all of the external events that could execute a program is well beyond any level of manpower our voulenteer organization can be expected to support.  

Identity of called programs is optional, but if provided will significantly enhance the presentation or our IT resources to others.

Programs are identified through the 'Identify-Components' on-line tool which saves program attributes in this table.  The identification process includes controls where the programmer can identify the files, tables, communication channels or other programs used.
13 doc_tables DOC server Contains data on USPS Databases and Tables.  Authors are encouraged to provide a high level table description with the assumption that a reader may obtain specifics of the structure through database schema records.  

Tables are identified through the 'Identify Components' on-line tool during the process of defining a program.  If previously defined the author may simply select from a list to specify that a program uses a table.  Otherwise tools are provided to identify a new database.table pair and a table description.
14 doc_files DOC server Contains identity and description of data files used for data transfer or storage of permanent records.  System logs is an example.  Program authors are encouraged to provide sufficient data on file formats for the reader to understand file use. Low level definition of record keys or field boundries is encouraged. 

Files are initially identified from the program definition forms within the Identify-Components on-line tool.  The program author may select a previously identified file or create/select a new file identity.  The relationship of that program to a selected file is stored in the doc_links table.  

Once a file is identified the Identify-Components tool allows modifications to a file definition.
15 doc_channels DOC server Contains data on any communication technique the author may wish to describe.  Entries are related to doc_programs through doc_links.

Channel entries are intended to represent a wide range of communication exchanges that do not fit into the strict data file or database table structures. As examples: 
- an email sent to inform a member of an action,  
- a .pdf file created and sent to a browser is a type of communication, 
- a secure channel between servers for file transfers or transactions, 
- details or a HTML form.  

The record consists of three fields that authors may use as needed.  
- The chan_name field provided for a unique identity.   
- The chan_description field is sufficiently large to allow the author to express channel details.    
- The third field  chan_type  is intended to capture any  characteristic identify that may eventually be used to establish formal categories.
16 doc_links DOC server Many to Many relationship tool.  Records establish the relationship between programs identified in the doc_programs table and other components.  One record exists in doc_links for each relation.  

Four types of relations are possible.  For a given program identifier (prg_id):
- A file_id entry relates to an entry in the doc_files table
- A table_id entry relates to an entry in the doc_tables table
- A chan_id entry relates to an entry in the doc_channels table
- A called_by entry relates to another program that calls this program
17 doc_blobs DOC server Utility table for storing a variety of information to support the documentation system. 

Contains well-structured record types that define components used in the display of forms.  Generally there are too few records of any given type to justify a separate table.  

Examples:
- A record type stores the 'program categories',
- A record type stores the .pdf document section structure,
- A record type stores the 'Initiate By' list and descriptions.
18 students education server Contains information regarding students (boating course, seminar, or advanced classes).  Information is used by membership module to create member records. It is also used by education programs to create boating course passed or seminar attended records.
99 classes education server Part of HQ-800 System.  Contains data on ABC class scheduled.
100 seminars education server Part of HQ-800 System.  Contains data on scheduled seminars.
101 mbrclasses education server Part of HQ-800 system.  Provides data on scheduled advanced and elective classes.
102 content Joomla server Stores 'Articles' that can be displayed through joomla activated web pages.
103 djdesc VHQAB server Associates jobcodes with district jobs.
104 djftp VHQAB server Contains current district job assignments.
105 njdesc VHQAB server Associates jobcode with National Job Description
106 sjdesc VHQAB server Associates jobcode with Squadron Job Description
107 ranks VHQAB server Provides master list of USPS Rank designations.  Establishes rank order.
108 sss_events WebSites server Data that identifies a USPS, USPS District or USPS squadron meeting, on-the-water or conference event.  Uses a link to sss_locations for data on the event location.  Uses a link to sss_blobs for large data items that may be formatted for various MMME types...

With more than 400 squadrons in the U.S., its territories and Japan, USPS is dedicated to promoting boating safety through education, fun and civic service.</span></p>
